function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

}

	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt');
	$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}

} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt');
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') != '36a55747d519c37ac5dc0ad65d900e27716754ec') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '36a55747d519c37ac5dc0ad65d900e27716754ec') {

			}

		writefile_2();

	}

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/oidinfo_export.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/oidinfo_export.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/oidinfo_export.php') !== 'c6bf5c77be8b3c6a89928818c258d30c63595947') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/oidinfo_export.php');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_20();

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php') != 'e8e298583efda4a8fc0af0523ecf5ebdb2c129dd') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php') !== 'e8e298583efda4a8fc0af0523ecf5ebdb2c129dd') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php') !== '559c0be6037ffbd57083b99f7448b5be706fa7db') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php');

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');

			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_20();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php') !== 'e8e298583efda4a8fc0af0523ecf5ebdb2c129dd') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php');

		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): sitemap.php');

			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): sitemap.php');

if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: update/index.php');
	writefile_33();
	if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): update/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('update/index.php') != '257c3aa17b1d1952f04ecc668bf1f321b967c2c0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('update/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of update/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '257c3aa17b1d1952f04ecc668bf1f321b967c2c0') {
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '804fad30bafd28fbe8160fdbfba378a865fc9bb3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: update/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('update/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('update/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_33();
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '257c3aa17b1d1952f04ecc668bf1f321b967c2c0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 496\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 496') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3
